To be able to fully perform the above tasks, the Test lead will need to work independently, but in close relationship with the requirement owners, maintenance team and stakeholders (internal and external).

 

The location is Stockholm.

 

Specific Competence

Job description: Cloud architect to new Cloud Office organization, Stockholm

We are looking for a cloud architect to join our Cloud Center of Excellence (called H&M Cloud Office) to help drive cloud adoption and onboarding across the entire H&M Group.

We are looking for a cloud architect to join our Cloud Center of Excellence to provide H&M IT with cutting edge cloud architecture, pushing the H&M group into the driver seat of IT development.

 

Get the opportunity to work inside our newly established Cloud Center of Excellence called H&M Cloud Office – a new unit supporting the entire H&M Group by spear-heading cloud adoption. You will, as a cloud architect, be working with cutting edge cloud technology, act as a Cloud Office representative and trusted advisor helping and guiding business units and development teams in their cloud-based initiatives. The overall ambition for Cloud Office is to fundamentally shift and improve the developer experience by applying emerging cloud technologies and tools. We are looking for a person who has a strong technical background along with good communication- and interpersonal networking skills. You are customer centric, have the ability to understand the business context of an application and the value provided of cloud-based solutions.

 

You are a team player with solid experience from cloud-based architecture and development. Your deep experience in cloud technologies and architecture will help project teams and initiatives in realizing an innovative and enterprise grade cloud solution architecture.

 

Your responsibilities The job as a cloud architect at H&M comes with a lot of responsibility – and lots of fun.

Your to do-list includes:

*	Be a part of the Cloud Office Adoption team that advises and support new cloud-based development initiatives and rearchitecting of existing applications to leverage cloud native patterns.
*	Ensuring and enabling fast paced, high quality development activities and cloud adoption for our internal customers, building success stories for H&M.
*	Seek feedback from stakeholders, capture stakeholder’s demand and facilitate the prioritization of development
*	Quantify cloud value and benefits in collaboration with Cloud Office colleagues and external stakeholders
*	Build strong and long-lasting relationships between the Cloud Office organization and external stakeholders.

 

Your skills

Just like everyone in Cloud Office, we believe you are a social, open, communicative, and ambitious team player full of drive and optimism.

Your skills include:

*	Deep technological skills and experience from IT architecture, development, operations and security
*	Experience of DevOps, continuous integration/continuous deployment and experience from agile environments (e.g. SAFe, Scrum)
*	Solid and hands on experience in cloud technologies, cloud architecture, and development
*	Strong communication and interpersonal networking skills, ability to build relationships on both executive and developer level
*	Structured approach and being comfortable in documenting a recommended solution architecture

 

Technology Skills

*	Cloud technologies with focus on Microsoft Azure and preferably deep in PaaS
*	Azure DevOps (former VSTS)
*	Azure Automation
*	Kubernetes
*	Docker
*	Serverless architectures

Nu söker vi en Mobile App Developer for IoT. 

ROLL: Mid-level Android/iOS App Developer

OM FÖRETAGET: 

At XX we have an obsessively strong customer focus. We have a profound commitment to deliver the highest quality solutions to help shape the life of our customers for the better. This requires us to deeply understand our customers, explore better ways to meet their needs and constantly verify our ideas with the real world.

The XX Group Design (EGD) within the Major Appliances Group is situated at our Head Quarters on Kungsholmen in Stockholm. As Design we are central to the creation of new products in XX, and work directly with R&D, software- and product development as well as balancing input and strategy from our business and marketing departments.

We offer a dynamic environment where you’ll have freedom to take initiative, opportunities for achieving personal growth and professional development. We truly acknowledge that it is the talent of our employees that sets us apart as the most customer- and experience focused leader in the cooking industry.

 

ARBETSUPPGIFTER:

Co-designing and developing Apps for both Android and iOS

- working with the Design Department on new features and prototyping designs for apps and connected appliances.

You will be responsible design and development of new features & prototypes for our mobile UI’s for both Android and iOS platforms, working together with the UX/UI-team within XX Group Design.

As a software developer within the UX/UI-team you’ll be actively involved throughout the entire interface development process. From user research, design and idea-generation to conceptualization, testing and implementation.

You’ll be working with a variety of stakeholders, both within our departments and outside. For instance User Researchers, Interaction-, Visual- and Industrial Designers to Hardware Engineers, Product Owners and Project Managers.

 

KOMPETENSKRAV:

The home appliance market domain is increasingly fast paced and is today being influenced by many other areas of the consumer electronic market. The UX/UI-team works and creates deliverables across a broad spectrum – both in terms of technology and products.

Therefore, with your background, we believe that you should…

Possess a Computer Science or Software engineering degree

Should have min 3 yrs of experience developing for iOS and Android, with good knowledge about Swift for iOS and Java/Kotlin for Android.

UI/UX development experience, knowing the Apple/Android guidelines, using Storyboards, auto layout, constraints (via UI and code)

Have a solid understanding of Object-oriented programming, Design Patterns, and Test Driven Development;

Great English language skills, other languages always a bonus.

Version control, specifically:

Git

Gradle in case of Android

Jenkins

Apple/Google Developer account setup (apps, certificates, profiles), how to configure an application, push notifications, how to upload and maintain a production app (have at least 2 or 3 released applications) 

 

Realm/Core Data/SQLite: Solid knowledge about local storage/persistence and how to optimize and safely work with it;

 

Hybrid App Frameworks

PhoneGap

Xamarin

Sencha

React

 

That’s why we believe that you as a person… 

are comfortable with being responsible for a tech area.

are self going, with a pro-active work attitude and ability to organize personal work to meet deadlines. 

are creative, energetic and inspire others.

dare to innovate and propose new solutions and approaches, also challenging existing ones.

Ämne:	ITC söker en UX-designer till Riksgälden #22-2019


ITC söker en UX-designer till Riksgälden


Period


2019-03-01 – 2019-06-30, möjlig förlängning till 2019-08-31


Omfattning


100%


Placeringsort


Stockholm


Beskrivning


Riksgälden
Riksgälden ska tillsammans med Finansdepartementet, Finansinspektionen och Riksbanken verka för att det finansiella systemet är stabilt. Det är ett viktigt ansvar eftersom en allvarlig störning i systemet kan orsaka stora kostnader för samhällsekonomin i form av svag tillväxt och ökad arbetslöshet.
Riksgäldens huvudsakliga uppdrag inom finansiell stabilitet är att hantera banker i kris och ansvara för insättningsgarantin.
Läs mer på www.riksgalden.se.

Stödjande IT-miljö
Riksgäldens webbplats, riksgalden.se syftar till att upprätta och förstärka förtroendet för Riksgälden hos allmänheten, investerare och återförsäljare.

Riksgalden.se hanterar information kring:

*	Privat- och företagssparare 
*	Myndigheter 
*	Investerare 
*	Om Riksgälden och vårt uppdrag 
*	Insättningsgarantin 

Webbplatsen är uppbyggd med hjälp av EpiServer CMS Epi9 med sökmotor EpiFind.
Webbplatsen hämtar information från ett antal externa källor via framförallt webservices.
Det finns även integrationer som går åt andra hållet, d.v.s. information insamlat från webben sparas i externa system.
Webbplatsen är uppbyggd av ASP.NET Webbforms framförallt bestående av Web pages (.aspx) och User controls (.ascx).


Uppdraget

Inledning
Kommunikationsenheten är systemägare till riksgalden.se och ska tillsammans med IT-avdelningen utveckla nuvarande version av EpiServer CMS 9 som idag endast är anpassad för desktop. Vi ska utveckla lösningen för en responsiv design för laptop, pekskärm och mobil som uppfyller webbtillgänglighet enligt WCAG 2.1.

Uppdraget innebär att anpassa layout och funktioner till en responsiv webbplats, inte att bygga en ny webbplats. Riksgälden ska även se över allt innehåll på webbplatsen som ska presenteras på ett mer användarvänligt och SEO-optimerat sätt.

Uppdraget ska leverera en interaktionsdesign som beskriver verksamhets- och målgruppsanalysen, interaktionen som äger rum mellan användarna och systemet, hur informationen i systemet ska struktureras och presenteras. Exempel på arbetsuppgifter är att ta fram skisser på hur användargränssnittet ska vara utformat för både laptop, pekskärm och mobil lösning.

Konsulten ska kunna ansvara för att nödvändiga användbarhetsaktiviteter genomförs i projektet utifrån funktioner, användarflöden, struktur och interaktion. Att kunna visualisera koncept och gränssnittsförslag för hur webbplatsen kan fungera.

Uppdraget sker tillsammans med Riksgäldens egna utvecklare och verksamhetsrepresentanter, där du justerar, kompletterar, kravställer och prioriterar i vilken ordning funktioner ska arbetas fram hela tiden med tillgänglighetskraven i beaktande.

Interaktionsdesignen och den grafiska formen ligger till grund för programmeringen av gränssnittet.
Under tiden för uppdraget ska konsulten även följa Riksgäldens miljörutiner.


Arbetssätt och Leveranskontroll
Konsulten för uppdraget ska följa Riksgäldens projekt- och utvecklingsmetodik. Riksgälden har en egenutvecklad metodik löst baserad på Pejl och DSDM/Agila manifestet.
Konsulten kommer att arbeta nära olika delar av verksamheten såsom affärsverksamheten, kommunikatörer, utvecklare, arkitekter, testare, säkerhets- och integrationsspecialister med flera.
Kontroll av leveranserna och dess fortskridande kommer att ske löpande under implementationen i form av utvärderingar efter varje ”timebox” och inom ramen för Riksgäldens projekt- och utvecklingsmetodik.

Säkerhetsklassning
Uppdraget är placerat i säkerhetsklass 3, det innebär att Riksgälden kommer att genomföra en registerkontroll av konsulten.


Kompetenskrav på konsult

SKA- och BÖR-krav:

Utbildning, certifiering eller diplomering

*	Konsulten BÖR vara certifierad eller diplomerad inom användbarhet. 

Erfarenhet

*	Konsulten SKA ha erfarenhet av implementering av tillgänglighetskrav enligt WCAG. 
*	Konsulten SKA ha erfarenhet av framtagande av interaktionsdesign. 
*	Konsulten SKA ha erfarenhet av innehålls- och strukturarbete utifrån responsiv design. 
*	Konsulten SKA ha tagit fram responsiva lösningar för webb tillsammans med beställare. Ange var och när i tid uppdragen utfördes. 

Språk

*	Konsulten SKA behärska svenska språket både skriftlig och muntligt. 
*	Konsulten BÖR behärska engelska språket både skriftlig och muntligt. 

Erfarenhet av kravarbete

*	Konsulten BÖR ha erfarenhet av arbete med kravarbete efter modeller såsom till exempel listor med krav, användningsfall eller user stories. 
*	Konsulten BÖR ha utvecklat och kommunicerat prototyper tillsammans med kund/beställare/kravställare. 

Erfarenhet av tekniker och produkter från Microsoft och EpiServer

*	Konsulten SKA ha erfarenhet av uppdrag eller projekt med utvecklare för webbapplikationer. 
*	Konsulten BÖR ha tagit fram lösningar för Episerver CMS version 8 eller senare, dokumenterat genom exempel på projekt och arbetsuppgifter. 
*	Konsulten BÖR ha arbetat fram interaktionslösningar som bygger på ASP.NET Webforms, dokumenterad erfarenhet genom exempel på projekt och arbetsuppgifter utförda någon gång under de senaste 5 åren. 
*	Konsulten BÖR ha erfarenhet av HTML5/CSS. 


Personliga egenskaper:
Pedagogisk förmåga, förståelse, lyhörd, flexibel och god kommunikationsförmåga på svenska.

Anbudsutvärdering:

Vid Riksgäldens anbudsutvärdering kommer endast de avropssvar som uppfyller alla obligatoriska SKA-krav att utvärderas.

Utvärderingen viktas enligt följande:

1.	Timpris (60%) 
2.	Kompetens (40%)

Ämne: meOneförfrågan för H&M, RITM0441900-0001 Contract Manager, F&A - SA

 

Hi, 

We are looking for a Contract Manager to F&A - SA, within BSF 

Level: B and C 
CV review: w.49--> 
Interviews: w.50--> 

You are welcome to send your prospects towards this RITM-number. 


Resource Request

________________________________


Number of resources requested: 1
Profile/Role: Contract Manager
Competence (consulting experience from the desired role and competence):
- B: 5-10 years
- C: >10 years
Utilization: 100%
DIVISION: Division Business Support Functions
Time reporting object: F&A - SA
Location: Stockholm
Period from: 2019-01-02
Period to: 2019-06-30

Job description:
Sourcing Responsible & Contract Manager to the IT Division BSF

 We are looking for a Sourcing Responsible / Contract Manager to one off our delivery areas, Finance & Accounting.

This role is based within the delivery area Finance & Accounting (size is 100+ people). The Sourcing Responsible/Contract Manager role is part of the delivery area management team (Delivery Responsible, Staff Responsible and Area Architects) and works closely with them in all matters relating to steering the delivery area. You will also work closely with System Responsibles and Project Managers to support them in the journey towards the right sourcing option. This is an exciting and challenging role where you will be a part of a dynamic delivery organization and a network of colleagues.

At BSF we are working in a successful offshore model with offshore partners represented in our delivery areas. You will work closely with their onsite leaders to improve our collaboration, with focus on excellent deliveries. You will be responsible for change management activities relating to our way of working with and steering our vendors.   

As a Sourcing Responsible your main focus is working with strategic and tactical plans and to secure that we use the right sourcing to be able to meet future challenges. You will assure that we have the best collaboration with our vendors and offshore partners as well as coach and lead other leaders within the area in these aspects.

As a Contract Manager your main focus will be to lead and support the contract lifecycle. You will assure that we follow the vendor management process, and that we steer and follow up on contracts with our vendors

To succeed in this roles, you need to be able to see the big picture and produce sourcing strategies and tactical sourcing plans that go hand in hand with our strategic delivery goals. You are a senior leader with proven communication skills, a strong personal drive and integrity. You like to work in a high pace environment with other strong leaders. You are business minded and experienced in procurement processes. You also have substantial experience from an IT environment with complex systems and a good understanding of different IT roles and Managed Service models.

Your responsibilities as Sourcing Responsible

*	Responsible for all sourcing of services and products, within the F&A delivery area.
*	Steering, support and follow-up of the implementation of sourcing strategies.
*	Driving change management activities
*	Coach and support leaders in defining the right scope for a service, how to evaluate vendor’s proposals, how to follow up and measure a service and collaborate with vendors.
*	Close cooperation with our vendors
*	Participating in the constant improvement and development of the sourcing function
*	Cooperation with other sourcing roles at the division and our central sourcing organization
*	Steering, support and follow-up of ongoing procurements

Your responsibilities as Contract Manager

*	Support and advice delivery situations with contract interpretation and discussions with existing vendors/contracts
*	Proactively aim to optimize existing contract conditions including active cost management (buy “more for less” and “buy the right amount of the right things”)
*	Initiate contract changes when relevant
*	Manage contractual and commercial risks and to ensure H & M’s and the vendor’s compliance with the agreement.
*	Lead and support the contract lifecycle (from contract is signed to termination of the contract) and be involved in the procurement process to gain relevant knowledge when relevant
*	Ensure good relations with our vendors and proactively work towards cooperation with our vendors so that commercial disputes are not influenced on delivery level.
*	Sometimes act as Procurement Lead for procurements within the service area.
*	Sometimes mentor other Procurement Leads.

Your skills

Just like everyone at H&M, we believe you are a social, open, communicative sales-minded and ambitious team player full of drive and optimism.

And your skills include:

*	Documented experience of at least 3 years of management roles within IT.
*	Minimum 2 years of IT purchasing, leading negotiations or contract management experience including experience in pricing models, payment plans and cost spend management
*	You have experience of working with external suppliers of IT services, IT systems and products, including offshore vendors or partners.
*	You have substantial experience from an IT environment with complex systems
*	You have experience of strategic planning, change management and practical implementation of new ways of working
*	Experience from working in an international environment
*	Very good skills in Swedish and English, both spoken and in writing

Work environment
Our IT office in Marievik is activity based environment and all consultants are expected to work Activity Based and understand this type of workplace.
